Modern Deck Lists, M-R
======================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on September 4, 2011 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











Pro Tour Philadelphia featured the debut of the Modern Constructed format. Listed below are players with last names starting with M-R who did not record 18 points or more during the 10 rounds of Modern.


For more deck lists, check out these links:


* [Top 8 Decks](http://archive.wizards.com/magic/magazine/article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptphi11/top8decklists)
* [Modern Deck Lists, 18 Points or Better](http://archive.wizards.com/magic/magazine/article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptphi11/topmoderndecks)
* Other Modern Deck Lists: [A-E](/en/articles/archive/event-coverage/modern-deck-lists-e-2011-09-04) | [F-L](/en/articles/archive/event-coverage/modern-deck-lists-f-l-2011-09-04) | [M-R](http://archive.wizards.com/magic/magazine/article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptphi11/decksmr) | [S-Z](http://archive.wizards.com/magic/magazine/article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptphi11/deckssz)







#### Seth Manfield
